<resp>{'time': 1602265171176, 'text': 'Sorry you did not enjoy our prices, we provide an "a la carte" service, because some of our clients would rather avoid additional heat after a treatment or wash, and we share the sentiment since too much heat could dry out the effects of certain treatments. However, we always want it to be an option for clients who need to be dry in a hurry.\nIf you have the time during your next appointment, requesting to finish under the dryer, rather than requesting an active blow dry service is no extra charge and provides gentler heat circulation then active drying. Neither service provides a bone straightening effect, as the amount of heat that would be needed to achieve such a thing would unavoidably cause some level of damage and hair health is our primary concern.\n\nAs for consultations, we do provide in person consults only, as it is difficult to understand the hair needs over the phone. For hair, visual and even physicals confirmation, is always the best to avoid unnecessary precautions that could hinder rather then help and we would like to avoid giving advice or precautions that could lead to more harm then good.\n\nI hope you find this response satisfactory and helpful when booking your next service.'}</resp><user_id>114983898501773642739</user_id>< Name>
NOT THAT SAVED YET< /Name>
< time>
1548017441801<//time>
<gmapID>0x80c2b8e049165691:0xd36dccc0e82dde0c</gmapID><Pics>None<//Pics>< text>
I enjoy the fact that Bebe's kids aren't running around like most black salons, the tea, the extremely comfortable shampoo chairs and the hair steam treatment. I don't enjoy the prices. I do appreciate quality but I don't like feeling like I'm being nickel and dimed for everything. It blows my mind that a blow dry is not a part of the process. By the time you finish the steam treatment and ask for a blow dry (not even straight hair blow out...just to dry it) expect to spend at least $80 not including the tip. That's a bit much. Truthfully you're better off just going to Sally's and buying a steamer for your home use. I'd recommend the products at LuLus but not the services. I too was informed after the consultation that I never got about the wet bar situation. Not cool. I tried to get a phone consultation. < text>
If I could give negative stars I would. I was sooo excited and ready to fall in love with this place.  I thought I found my new salon home. Organic Black Hair Salon,  so LA, so amazing,  like finding a needle in a haystack!

All the ambiance and organic products don't mean anything if you can't/don't thoroughly communicate your services to a new client.

For one,  it should be called a "wet bar" since ALL the employees are too oblivious to communicate to NEW clients that if you want your hair dried, that they have to factor in time for that in your appointment.

And if they're about to close, they will have you walk out with a fully wet head [even though you communicate repeatedly YOU would NEVER do that] bc they can't be bothered to dry your hair bc they want to go home. REALLLY?!

You don't think it's IMPORTANT to communicate that to a brand new client who asked for a consultation BEFORE you wet their massive thick head of hair [they told you they always wear their hair straight]?!?!

And then there's 30 minutes left until "closing time"& you'd rather argue with the client over a technicality, instead of righting the wrong.  And then the manager comes in and commences to argue with me about how I can leave with a wet head and come back another day at their convenience.  So now instead of wasting 30 minutes of my time,  you've now wasted OVER an hour about how you "can't".

In the hour they spent arguing with me,  thru could've been drying my hair!

Sadly,  this is one of the reasons why so many black owned businesses do not thrive.  As a business owner, don't argue with a customer.  Take full accountability for YOUR STAFF being UNCLEAR,  by not communicating to a new customer how their salon works.  It's YOUR responsibility to 'dummy proof' any new client to properly manage expectations.  YOU give the client ALL of the information they need so they can make  FULLY INFORMED decision prior to receiving services.  Don't refer to your staff's LACK of communication as "client/staff 'miscommunication'". And right the wrong at the client's convenience, not yours.

I shell out tons of money for my hair, I shouldn't have to argue to pay someone to finish doing my damn hair.

I was ready to arrange a whole day with me and my gfs to go and have the place to ourselves. Instead,  I'm writing a review after driving home,  pissed and staying up 2 hours untangling, drying,  and straightening my own hair. #Wasteoftime< /text>

< text>
I Hate Lulu's
I went in to get a root coloring (greys); A trim and deep conditioning. First off, on a positive note, it's a lovely atmosphere. Clean facility and soothing music. BUT IT ENDS THERE
I was met by a cosmetology STUDENT who informed me that she was still working on her HOURS (!!???) I regret stopping services not because she wasn't African American BUT because she told me that she was a "work in progress"...SMH--Who wants a work in progress working on their head? I mean these are a la carte  salon prices. $65 for root coloring; $60 for cut; $35 for deep conditioning (which consists of olive oil added to conditioner and being place under a "steam machine"; $15 dollars for a blow dry (if you don't want your hair cut wet) $175 in total.
After the student colored my hair and conditioned my hair. The other services were performed by another young lady--who did the blow dry and cut (cut was not "precision" as advertised). It infuriates me that the second young lady in my head failed to inform me that the grays (that she watched the student cover) were still very visible.
I left looking like I just wasted my money; Got home to have braids put in and was told that I had a head full of grays. I called and immediately returned to the shop to ask that the money I spent for the color be returned. THIS IS WHERE I MET THE OWNER LULU.
When got there, a member of the staff went through my hair to confirm that my grays were not covered. The owner (Lulu) approached me, refused to give me back my money. I mean this woman had a smug (I'm the owner) attitude, literally making up excuses for her student worker ("I give people chances") and telling me her (coloring) product was made with natural ingredients--therefore "it doesn't always take on the first try".  After making it clear that my money would not be refunded, Lulu told me to come back and that she would do my hair HERSELF..."Please give me a chance to make it right" she says. Went back two days later, she colored my hair--this time placing me under a dryer with the color on (something the student skipped the first time). I left feeling less robbed than the first time but now that I washed my hair (first time since it got done) no color.

If you want to waste your money on procedures that you can do at home? Go to Lulu's. Otherwise, take heed.< /text>

< Text>
It's been awhile since I gave a 5 star review but this little hidden gem sure deserved it. I saw this fairly new place a week ago while running errands and stopped by for lunch with a friend today.
Since the menu classified the starters as tapas, we were going to order a few and then share a ramen or a sizzling bibimbab. The tapas were large in portions and we couldn't even finish the 4 we order. We thought we were done till they brought out the dessert menu.

Seafood Jeon $6.50
Korean savory pancake with mixed seafood
5* This was one of the best dishes, 2 small pancakes perfectly cooked. Crispy and tender at the same time.

Boneless Fried Chicken (spicy or soy garlic) $7.50
Bite size Korean style crispy boneless chicken with your choice of flavor
5* Another hit, chicken was cooked to perfection and the sauce was perfectly seasoned.

Popcorn Salmon $6
Bite size fried salmon with spicy
4* The salmon was just slightly overcooked for my liking but still divine.

Corn Cheese $6
Corn with creamy sauce and cheese on sizzling pan
3* This was average, nothing spectacular. Next time we will order the slicked beef salad instead.

I forgot to take a picture of the dessert, the Mango Panna Cotta was definetly a nice touch to end a delicious meal. I gave this restaurant 5 stars because the waitstaff was excellent. Great service with a smile!< /Text>

<GmapID>0x808587104f41f0c5:0xdcb394671cb8b32d<//GmapID><rating>2</rating><resp>None<//resp>< review>
Stopped in after seeing a recommendation from a friend and plenty of good reviews on here. I wanted to try the katsu-don but when I asked the waitress about it she said they could not make it that evening...so I decided to order the bulgogi bowl and some okonomiyaki fries.

I didn't expect the okonomiyaki fries ($6) to be good but actually they were excellent. The fries had a McDonald's like texture but gourmet with kewpie mayo and katsu sauce finished with bonito flakes on top. Excellent.

Then the bulgogi bowl ($12.95) appeared. This bowl was a sad bulgogi bowl with disappointing small slices of meat that tasted like every Korean AYCE BBQ place I've ever been to. There was tons of green salad (with no dressing) and rice that filled the whole bowl probably at least 80% of the bowl with some clear noodles.

I would much rather pay more and have good bulgogi than pay less and have a disappointing experience. The bulgogi marinade was also super sweet, acid reflux inducing...overall just not good. I would not order it again.

The ambiance is nice here and its a good place to go with friends and maybe order some tapas, but if you really love Korean food you might find yourself disappointed at Jijime.<//review>

< review>
Quaint little campgrounds.  Close to town for supplies. Pretty quiet during the week  but weekends can get busy. Vault toilets  dumpsters and there is water at half of the sites. Trees along the river act as a windbreak. Not all sites have shade. There are picnic tables and fire ring or BBQ stands at each site. The river drowns out most noises.  Dogs okay on a  leash. No on-site  host but someone comes by everyday to check the bathrooms and trash.< /review>

< text>
Cool campground. There are restrooms and drinking water, fire rings and seating places provided, no shower. We have seen, that the gast station close by hast showers to use, we haven't tried them. There is a small river flowing through the campground, awesome for a refreshing shower, but cold ;)
14$ per campground. Awesome view surrounds the campground.</text>

< review>
Beautiful little campground. Nice and clean. There is a little Creek running through it as you may have surmised by the name.. However it is not for large RV'S. Fortunately there weren't many campers and we could maneuver around the loop. There was one spot large enough for us, but since it's a one way in and one way out campground, it could have been tricky had it been more crowded. The view is absolutely gorgeous. I highly recommend this campground.< /review>

Great selection of retail stores and dining establishments. The theater, with several screens,  usually has something everyone would like to see. The Plant security is always patrolling, on foot or in a vehicle, and they are ready to help if you need them. The best part is that there's plenty of free parking. There is more then 7 different entrances to this shopping center. You do not need to get caught up in the In & Out Burger drive thru traffic.</Review>
